Pro Tour–Amsterdam Extended Decks A-F
=====================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on September 5, 2010 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











The following decks earned 17 or fewer points in the 10 rounds of Swiss play at Pro Tour-Amsterdam.

* [Top Extended Decks (18 points or higher)](http://archive.wizards.com/Magic/Magazine/Article.aspx?x=mtg/daily/eventcoverage/ptams10/topExtended)
* [Extended Decks, A-F](http://archive.wizards.com/Magic/Magazine/Article.aspx?x=mtg/daily/eventcoverage/ptams10/exta-f)
* [Extended Decks, G-L](http://archive.wizards.com/Magic/Magazine/Article.aspx?x=mtg/daily/eventcoverage/ptams10/extg-l)
* [Extended Decks, M-R](http://archive.wizards.com/Magic/Magazine/Article.aspx?x=mtg/daily/eventcoverage/ptams10/extm-r)
* [Extended Decks, S-Z](http://archive.wizards.com/Magic/Magazine/Article.aspx?x=mtg/daily/eventcoverage/ptams10/exts-z)
